             <icon aria-busy="false" aria-hidden="true" class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon lazy-loaded" data-tracking-will-navigate="">
              <svg aria-busy="false" class="lazy-loaded" data-supported-dps="24x24" fill="currentColor" focusable="false" height="24" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
               <path d="M21 8H8a1 1 0 00-1 1v10a1 1 0 001 1h10l4 3V9a1 1 0 00-1-1zm-1 11.11L18.52 18H9v-8h11v9.11zM12 15h5v1h-5v-1zm-8-2h1v2H3a1 1 0 01-1-1V4a1 1 0 011-1h13a1 1 0 011 1v2h-2V5H4v8zm14 0h-7v-1h7v1z">

         <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
          <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
           <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5 relative overflow-hidden">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Responsibilities:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              To understand business requirements in the BI context and design data models to convert raw data to meaningful insights.
             </li>
             <li>
              To create dashboards and visual interactive reports using Power BI.
             </li>
             <li>
              To identify KPIs with clear objectives and monitor them consistently.
             </li>
             <li>
              To analyze data and present it through reports that can help in decision-making.
             </li>
             <li>
              To be able to convert business requirements into technical specifications and decide the timeline to accomplish tasks.
             </li>
             <li>
              To design, develop, and deploy Power BI scripts and perform efficient detailed analysis.
             </li>
             <li>
              To perform DAX queries and functions in Power BI.
             </li>
             <li>
              To create charts and document data with algorithms, parameters, models, and relations explanations.
             </li>
             <li>
              To conduct data warehouse development.
             </li>
             <li>
              To perform SQL querying for best results.
             </li>
             <li>
              To use filters and graphs for a better understanding of the data.
             </li>
             <li>
              To define and design new systems by analyzing current ETL processes.
             </li>
             <li>
              To make technical changes to existing BI systems in order to enhance their working.
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Requirements:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              4 to 8 years of experience working in Data Visualization and Solutions.
             </li>
             <li>
              Expert in Power BI data analysis, data visualization, writing DAX, and building dashboards and reports.
             </li>
             <li>
              Expertise in designing and developing a semantic layer of BI Tools.
             </li>
             <li>
              Collect, refine, and prepare data for analytics and visualization. Manage and utilize the Power BI platform to extract meaningful insights from it.
             </li>
             <li>
              Prepare reports using various visualization and data modeling methods. Define new KPIs and consistently measure them in the datasets.
             </li>
             <li>
              Develop, manage and enhance data models across key metrics to provide best-in-class, transparent and accurate forecasting.
             </li>
             <li>
              Partner with the business leaders and end-user base exercising flexibility in a matrixed organization to identify emerging trends and implement meaningful drivers.
             </li>
             <li>
              Ability to process large amounts of data to identify key drivers and develop robust models for various types of analysis and communicate effectively to stakeholders.
             </li>
             <li>
              Ability to write SQL queries and stored procedures. Familiarity with various relational database platforms (SQL Server, Teradata, Oracle, Snowflake, Vertica, etc).
             </li>
             <li>
              Strong communication skills.
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <br/>
            </p>
            <p>
             Location: Lahore/Karachi/Islamabad/Multan/Faisalabad
            </p>
           </div>
